(Multi-play games are offered in \"Triple Play\", \"Five Play\", \"Ten Play\", \"Fifty Play\" and \"One Hundred Play\" versions.) \r\n\r\nIn games which do not have a wild card a player on average will receive the rare four-of-a-kind hand approximately once every 500 hands, while a player may play tens of thousands of hands before an extremely rare royal flush, which usually has the highest payout. \r\n\r\n\"Jacks or Better,\" sometimes simply called \"Draw Poker,\" is the most common variation of video poker. Usually, every article gets reviewed in a period of 12 hours.\r\n\r\nIf your article doesn’t get published or approved, then it may contain poor quality content.\r\n\r\nHere are some minimum requirements for publishing content with Blogmaza:\r\n• We don’t accept any type of content that may look like spam, promotional, or advertising.\r\n• We do allow external links to some extent but we will disallow links that may feel unnecessary.\r\n• If you are guest posting, we will allow a link back to your content to some extent if it meets our standards.\r\n• Each content you write must cover the topic in details, uncovered topics and half written content will be rejected.\r\n• Your article must be unique and of minimum 500 words, any type of copywriting is not allowed.\r\n• Your grammar must be correct, and the language and choice of words must be easy to understand.\r\n• Infographics, images, and videos are always welcome; but if it is not created by you, you must give credit to its author.\r\n• Only content that resembles our main topics are allowed, any other type is content will be rejected.\r\n• You must reply to comments on your articles whenever necessary.\r\n\r\nPost Formats:\r\n• Personality quiz\r\nSeries of questions that intends to reveal something about the personality\r\n• Trivia quiz\r\nSeries of questions with right and wrong answers that intends to check knowledge\r\n• Poll\r\nVoting to make decisions or determine opinions\r\n• Story\r\nFormatted Text with Embeds and Visuals\r\n• List\r\nThe Classic Internet Listicles\r\n• Open List\r\nSubmit your own item and vote up for the best submission\r\n• Ranked List\r\nUpvote or downvote to decide the best list item\r\n• Countdown\r\nThe Classic Internet Countdowns\r\n• Meme\r\nUpload your own images to make custom memes\r\n• Video\r\nUpload Your Videos or Youtube, Vimeo or Vine Embeds\r\n• Audio\r\nMP3 or Soundcloud or Mixcloud Embeds\r\n• Image\r\nPhoto or GIF\r\n• Gif\r\nGIF Images\r\n\r\nRead More: https://www.blogmaza.com/become-a-blogger/\r\n\r\nSo, why wait?
